< review>
Came here for the first time with a buddy after a relatively long bike ride. In other words, I was starving and, if required, would do anything for food at that point. I ordered the cheesesteak sandwich, which comes open face, and a tall Coors Light (yeah, I know Coor's Light, but it was hot day and we were on bikes so it was perfect). My buddy claimed they only serve beers in liters. Whether he was lying to me or not, I still opted for the giant beer mug.

Anyways, back to the food. As I mentioned, I was starving and - sure - I would have eaten almost anything. BUT I honestly can say that this sandwich was simply amazing. The meat was tender, the bread was delicious, the cheese was melty ... it just worked. I don't live in Oceanside but I can say that I'll be back. #Truth< /review>

< Review>
Unsung is located right next to the packing district.  I've been coming here for years. Pre-COVID it was an awesome to hang out, drink a beer, grab a board game, and chill. Lots of cool decor inside from comics, star wars, and other sci fi. Beers are consistently solid, and I love the naming conventions that match the vibe of the place. I love supporting this place, and they have offered solid takeout options from 4 packs to different crowler sizes. Easily one of my favorite breweries in Orange County.<//Review>

<text>Great spot with great beers!  Awesome location by the Packing District.

On my first trip here I didn't know they only fill in stainless steel growlers. Lots of places advertise their growler fill policy on their website; it would be nice if they did this since they have one of the most restrictive policies on generic growlers. The only places that are more restrictive are the places that only fill their own, which are becoming very rare, thankfully!

If you want to bring your own growler for fills, it will need to be stainless steel. They "claim" the amber/dark glass growlers let in enough light to make their beer no longer taste right very quickly so they won't fill them.< /text>< name>

First time going here with my family, I order milk tea boba and it's delicious.
Staff service 5/5: the staff was nice to ask about signing up for the Square program. I like how they have a vibrating alert device to alert their customers that their drinks are ready to pick up.My first time seeing a boba place that have this feature.

Drinks 5/5: I ordered two Milk Tea with boba and the boba are chewy and warm. The drink isn't heavy in sweetness which is good. Not low on sweet nor high on sweet. So this would be great for anyone who are careful about their sugar level. The drinks are delicious.

Place 5/5: This spot is a good place to bring friends and family to hangout and have some drinks. Chill comfortable spot. Also this place has WiFi. Some customers work on their graphics design projects on their laptop, others do their homework, some play board games/card games.< /Text>

<Text>First, thank for staying open during the times indicated by your store hours even though there wasn't any business. SO many times I've driven to restaurants that are supposed to be open late but close early due to lack of customers .. So infuriating!

The owner served us and he was so patient in explaining our choices and what people usually like. I got the Korean pear with blueberry. They hand-squeeze the gel and use tweezers to put on each type of mint- WOW!  They make it look like an art form. It tasted like iced Korean pear, and the blueberry gave it more of a kick. They even had blueberries frozen inside! My favorite was the calpico gel though.. MmmMMm. It really tasted like calpico!

My boyfriend got the nutella and banana. It was REALLY good as well, and the sweetest bar they have (although it's not overwhelmingly sweet). So each bite consisted of this creamy banana, drizzle of nutella gel, and the crunch of the banana chips on top. REALLY good. And the banana tasted like a real banana, not some processed "fruit." We sampled the horchata ice cream too and it was so good as well. However, my dessert stomach isn't as big as my regular-food stomach, so I had to choose between ice cream or a bar.

BUT my boyfriend's dessert stomach is pretty big, so after getting his nutella and banana bar, he got one more. It was the mango and strawberry(?) one I believe.  It made my relive my lucas-eating childhood, where we would spend recesses trying to squeeze and eat all the lucas hairs out of those lucas containers. I really like how tangy this bar was, yet refreshing with the mango and strawberry base.

The d√©cor is really cool and hip. I liked the color scheme and how the bar stools are situated at different heights pertaining to the wall d√©cor. It gives off the same futuristic vibe as the ice cream lab. I KNOW this place is going to blow up soon, sooo come NOW before the line becomes regularly out the door!</Text><Pics>None<//Pics><response>None</response>< gmapID>

<gmap_id>0x80c2d7d5269d769d:0x6ce6f6d751bc2029<//gmap_id>< review>
I have been wanting to try The Ice Bar for quite awhile, and I finally was able to get the chance to try. While I think the bars definitely make a great photo-op, I don't think I would return often just because the prices are a little high and the location is quite far.

The storefront is very bright and welcoming. Lots of tables and chairs. The workers were friendly and explained to us the menu since we had never been to The Ice Bar before. You pick a pop, then choose if you want to eat it plain, in the way that The Ice Bar customizes it, or customize it yourself. There's different prices for each option.

I tried the Korean Pear Blueberry and Strawberry Lemonade House Style. Both of them were made in front of my eyes (ooh) and after taking a ton of pictures, I was able to try them both. They were interesting. I think the popsicle base reminded me of the ones I used to get from the street vendors or ice cream trucks when I was younger. But having all the fancy sauces and garnishes definitely give the popsicle base an extra kick. The Strawberry Lemonade was okay. I liked the Pop Rocks and the tanginess of the strawberry lemonade popsicle. I thought the Korean Pear Blueberry was much tastier. It was more refreshing and cool, a good treat on a hot day.

I think the total price was around $6-$7, a decent price for a first time ever gourmet popsicle experience. The popsicles were creamy and had good flavor, but I don't think I'd make the trip out to West Covina just to get an ice pop.

Just a side-note: check out the bathroom! The wall art is pretty cool :)</review>

<rating>1< /rating>< Review>
We have had a scheduled cleaning of our home every four weeks for a while now. The upside is when the maids are here, they do a good job.

But scheduling and consistency of showing up on time has been a nightmare. Worst customer experience of any business I've ever dealt with- and I say that with full seriousness, not being hyperbolic. I'm not someone who gives a negative review lightly.

They show up on time well below 50% of the time. They ask to reschedule less than an hour before the booking all the time. Multiple times we have caught them in an outright lie regarding their excuse about why they are late or can't make it. Multiple times I have done phone tag with their customer service and ran around my complex looking for maids who they say are there, only to find out a half hour later that they were never there in the first place.

I'm willing to be pretty accommodating with scheduling. But don't lie to me and intentionally waste my time. I feel bad for the actual cleaners since I somewhat suspect these issues are out of their hands, but I just can't keep giving this company my business.< /Review>

< text>
They are NOT "instant". The first time I used Instamaids everything was great as far as the service three women came and took care of everything in a little over an hour. The second time they forgot to clean my tub and I needed them to come out a second time to clean it. Didn't bother me mistakes happen and I let is slide but received no incentive for the mistake. This third time was a disaster. They were scheduled between 8am and 9am (today) but when we called they said they would call us back in 10 minutes. We did not hear back until 45 minutes later. The employees that were scheduled to clean my home were " in an accident" but this was failed to be reported to us and had we not called we would have never received this information.

I am just glad we did not have an important event in our home and relied on them to arrive. Their communication is not good. They make their own schedule and will leave you guessing on their arrival.

The worst of it is I am an Assistant Property Manager where I live and refer my residents to them and moving forward I will not be giving their information out. Lets just say, you may be happy the first time but they will fail you at some point. I suggest that instead of finding a company that is good IF they arrive you find another cleaning company that arrives when they say they will as well as do a good job.</text>
